            <script>
            var args = document.location.search.substring(1).split('&');
            argsParsed = {};
            for (var i = 0; i< args.length; i++) {
                var arg = decodeURIComponent(args[i]);
                if (arg.indexOf('=') == -1) {
                    argsParsed[arg.trim()] = true;
                } else {
                    var kvp = arg.split('=');
                    argsParsed[kvp[0].trim()] = kvp[1].trim();
                }
            }
            var aps = {};
            if (argsParsed.hasOwnProperty("s")) {
                aps.key = 'keyword';
                aps.values = argsParsed["s"].split('+');
            } else if (argsParsed.hasOwnProperty("tsp")) {
                 aps.key = 'keyword';
                 aps.values = ['top_story_page'];
            }
        </script>

		<div class="blogitem" id="post-68372" class="post-68372 post type-post status-publish format-standard hentry category-alec-baldwin blogentry">

	
				<h2 class="blogtitle">
					<a href="http://blog.sfgate.com/dailydish/2013/08/27/alec-baldwin-involved-in-incident-with-photographer/" title="Permalink to Alec Baldwin involved in incident with photographer" rel="bookmark">Alec Baldwin involved in incident with photographer</a>
				</h2>

						<div class="socialtools clearfix">

							</div>

</script></li><li class="share-twitter"><div class="twitter_button"><iframe allowtransparency="true" frameborder="0" scrolling="no" src="http://platform.twitter.com/widgets/tweet_button.html?url=http%3A%2F%2Fblog.sfgate.com%2Fdailydish%2F2013%2F08%2F27%2Falec-baldwin-involved-in-incident-with-photographer%2F&#038;counturl=http%3A%2F%2Fblog.sfgate.com%2Fdailydish%2F2013%2F08%2F27%2Falec-baldwin-involved-in-incident-with-photographer%2F&#038;count=horizontal&#038;text=Alec%20Baldwin%20involved%20in%20incident%20with%20photographer%3A" style="width:86px; height:20px;"></iframe></div></li><li class="share-google-plus-1"><div class="googleplus1_button"><div class="g-plusone" data-size="medium" data-callback="sharing_plusone" data-href="http://blog.sfgate.com/dailydish/2013/08/27/alec-baldwin-involved-in-incident-with-photographer/"></div></div></li><li class="share-end"></li></ul></div></div></div><div id="attachment_68373" class="wp-caption alignleft" style="width: 248px"><img src="http://blog.sfgate.com/dailydish/wp-content/blogs.dir/2247/files/2013/08/alec-238x300.jpg" alt="(Photo by Monica Schipper/FilmMagic)" width="238" height="300" class="size-medium wp-image-68373" /><p class="wp-caption-text">(Photo by Monica Schipper/FilmMagic)</p></div>
<p>Actor Alec Baldwin has been involved in another altercation with a photographer.</p>
<p>  The alleged incident occurred on Tuesday in New York and there are conflicting reports surrounding who the aggressor was.</p>
<p>  <a href="http://www.tmz.com/2013/08/27/alec-baldwin-nypd-photog-attack/" target="_blank">According to TMZ.com</a> and sources close to the couple, Baldwin and his wife Hilaria were grabbing something to eat when the shutterbug became overzealous.</p>
<p>  However, the photographer insists he did not approach the couple aggressively.</p>
<p>  He tells WENN, &#8220;I was taking video and asking questions. Ultimately I was doing my job.&#8221;</p>
<p>  Baldwin&#8217;s newborn daughter, Carmen Gabriela who was born on Friday, was not with the actor at the time of the incident.</p>
<p>  The actor and the photographer, who both admitted to pushing each other, have decided not to press charges and the police have reportedly closed the case.</p>
<p>  This isn&#8217;t Baldwin&#8217;s first run-in with paparazzi. In June, he was accused of hitting a photographer, after obtaining a marriage license in New York. </p>

<div class="ngggroup"></div>

<p>Superstar couple Beyonce and Jay Z got caught in the middle of a bust-up between Sean &#8220;Diddy&#8221; Combs and his rap pal J. Cole at an MTV Video Music Awards afterparty on Sunday.</p>
<p>Combs and Cole clashed following a heated exchange of words at the bash at New York&#8217;s Dream Hotel, and Jay Z had to intervene and pull the warring pair apart, according to the New York Daily News.</p>
<p>Cole, real name Jermaine Lamarr Cole, was escorted out of the building following the scuffle, but Combs later took to Twitter.com to play down the incident, dismissing it as a loud argument between two friends.</p>
<p>He writes, &#8220;I usually don&#8217;t address rumors but I got too much respect for my bro J. Cole. We are friends. We just yell in public sometimes.&#8221;</p>
<p>The red-and-black themed party was attended by a host of celebrities including Rita Ora, Jamie Foxx, will.i.am, Russell Simmons and Busta Rhymes.</p>
<p>More VMA 2013 coverage:</p>
<p><a href="http://blog.sfgate.com/dailydish/2013/08/25/mtv-vmas-2013-the-show-and-yes-nsync-reunited/" title="MTV VMAs 2013: The show (and yes, ‘NSYNC reunited!)" target="_blank">Show highlights</a></p>
<p><a href="http://blog.sfgate.com/dailydish/2013/08/26/mtv-vmas-2013-the-fashions/" title="MTV VMAs 2013: The fashions" target="_blank">The fashions</a></p>
<p><a href="http://blog.sfgate.com/dailydish/2013/08/25/mtv-vma-2013-red-carpet/" title="MTV VMA 2013: Red carpet" target="_blank">Red carpet<br />

		<div class="blogitem" id="post-68362" class="post-68362 post type-post status-publish format-standard hentry category-ricky-martin blogentry">

	
				<h2 class="blogtitle">
					<a href="http://blog.sfgate.com/dailydish/2013/08/27/ricky-martin-i-bullied-gay-people/" title="Permalink to Ricky Martin: &#8216;I bullied gay people&#8217;" rel="bookmark">Ricky Martin: &#8216;I bullied gay people&#8217;</a>
				</h2>

<p>Ricky Martin admits he was homophobic as he struggled to deal with his own sexuality.</p>
<p>  The superstar came out in 2010 after years of speculation. He has since become an outspoken advocate of gay rights around the world, but has revealed he would aim abuse at homosexuals while he tried to secretly deal with his feelings.</p>
<p>  In an interview with Australian GQ, he says, &#8220;I was very angry, very rebellious. I used to look at gay men and think, &#8216;I&#8217;m not like that; I don&#8217;t want to be like that, that&#8217;s not me.&#8217; I was ashamed.</p>
<p>  &#8220;When you&#8217;re told you&#8217;re wrong by everyone, from society, from your faith &#8211; my self-esteem was crushed. I took my anger out on those around me.</p>
<p>  &#8220;I look back now and realize I would bully people who I knew were gay. I had internalized homophobia. To realize that was confronting to me. I wanted to get away from that.&#8221; </p>

<p>Singer Demi Lovato is set to go gay for a cameo appearance on hit TV musical “Glee.”</p>
<p>  “The X Factor” judge will make a guest appearance on Ryan Murphy&#8217;s musical series, in which she will play a love interest for Naya Rivera&#8217;s lesbian character Santana Lopez.</p>
<p>  Leaking the news at the MTV Video Music Awards on Sunday, Rivera told Gossip Cop, &#8220;She&#8217;s playing my (character Santana&#8217;s) love interest so I&#8217;m very, very excited about that.</p>
<p>  &#8220;We get to sing a song together. &#8230; I&#8217;m excited to work with her. We&#8217;re bringing her to the dark side.</p>

<p>Miley Cyrus&#8217; former TV mom Brooke Shields took aim at the pop star for her provocative performance at the MTV Video Music Awards on Sunday night, saying the grown-up “Hannah Montana” star looked &#8220;desperate&#8221; onstage.</p>
<p>  Shields played Miley&#8217;s mom on the hit Disney show and her daughters, ages 6 and 10, are big fans, but the actress wasn&#8217;t impressed with her ex-co-star&#8217;s saucy routine at the Barclays Center in New York.</p>
<p>  The 20-year-old stripped down to her rubber underwear and donned a giant foam hand to perform “Blurred Lines” with Robin Thicke, who seemed more than a little bemused as his stage partner danced provocatively in front of him and grinded her backside into his crotch, while making inappropriate gestures to the audience.</p>
<p>  Shields was a co-host on “Today” on Monday and admitted she didn&#8217;t like what she saw.</p>
<p>  She joked, &#8220;I don&#8217;t approve. What did I do wrong?&#8221; Shields then got serious, adding, &#8220;I just want to know who is advising her and why it&#8217;s necessary (to do that). My 6-year-old and my 10-year-old, they can&#8217;t watch that.</p>
<p>  &#8220;She can sing beautifully, and I feel like if she lets that lead, rather than let her bottom lead. … I feel it&#8217;s a bit desperate &#8211; you&#8217;re trying to be (Lady) Gaga &#8230; but it&#8217;s different &#8230; She&#8217;s trying so, so hard.&#8221;</p>
<div id="attachment_68352" class="wp-caption alignright" style="width: 310px"><a href="http://blog.sfgate.com/dailydish/wp-content/blogs.dir/2247/files/2013/08/Miley-Cyrus1.jpg"><img src="http://blog.sfgate.com/dailydish/wp-content/blogs.dir/2247/files/2013/08/Miley-Cyrus1-300x199.jpg" alt="(Photo by Jeff Kravitz/FilmMagic for MTV) " width="300" height="199" class="size-medium wp-image-68352" /></a><p class="wp-caption-text">(Photo by Jeff Kravitz/FilmMagic for MTV)<br /></p></div>
<p>  But Shields gave her one-time TV daughter top marks for grabbing the headlines: &#8220;She went for it &#8230; and we&#8217;re all talking about her.&#8221;</p>
<p>  The actress wasn&#8217;t the only famous mom stunned by Miley&#8217;s moves: Thicke&#8217;s mother, singer Gloria Loring, was also confused by what the former child star was trying to achieve.</p>
<p>  She says, &#8220;I don&#8217;t understand what Miley Cyrus is trying to do. I think she&#8217;s misbegotten in this attempt of hers. And I think it was not beneficial. I didn&#8217;t get what her point was. It was so over the top as to almost be a parody of itself.&#8221; </p>
													</div><!-- .entry-content -->

<div class="ngggroup"></div>

<p>Funnymen Seth Rogen, Jonah Hill and Bill Hader led the bawdy tributes to their pal James Franco as the actor was &#8220;roasted&#8221; in California on Sunday night.</p>
<p>The star was the butt of all jokes at the Comedy Central Roast as his pals mocked his movie flops, his sexuality and his much-maligned co-hosting gig with Anne Hathaway at the 2011 Oscars.</p>
<p>Rogen, who served as master of ceremonies, held nothing back as he picked on his &#8220;Pineapple Express&#8221; co-star, quipping, &#8220;He once told me he worked for 36 hours straight, which I didn&#8217;t believe. The straight part, of course.&#8221;</p>
<p>According to TheWrap.com, the host also joked, &#8220;Look at me doing all the talking while you sit there doing nothing. I feel like I&#8217;m hosting the Oscars with you!&#8221;</p>
<p>But Franco was given some respite at the TV taping in Culver City when the comedy stars let rip at one another.</p>
<p>Poking fun at chubby actor Hill, Jeff Ross said, &#8220;When Jonah Hill&#8217;s agent told him Quentin Tarantino wanted him to be in a spaghetti western, Jonah said, &#8216;You had me at spaghetti.&#8217;&#8221;</p>
<p>Hill got his own back when he took aim at stand-up star Sarah Silverman, telling her, &#8220;You were one of my favorite comedians as a kid. I don&#8217;t get why people say she&#8217;s hot for a comic. She&#8217;s not hot for a comic, she&#8217;s hot for her age.&#8221;</p>
<p>Franco&#8217;s roast will air as a special on Comedy Central on Labor Day.</p>

</li><li class="share-email"><a rel="nofollow" class="share-email sd-button" href="http://blog.sfgate.com/dailydish/2013/08/26/kristin-chenoweth-stunned-by-talented-fan-at-hollywood-gig/?share=email" title="Click to email this to a friend"><span>Email</span></a></li><li class="share-print"><a rel="nofollow" class="share-print sd-button" href="http://blog.sfgate.com/dailydish/2013/08/26/kristin-chenoweth-stunned-by-talented-fan-at-hollywood-gig/" title="Click to print"><span>Print</span></a></li><li class="share-facebook"><a onclick="javascript: window.open('https://www.facebook.com/sharer/sharer.php?u=http%3A%2F%2Fblog.sfgate.com%2Fdailydish%2F2013%2F08%2F26%2Fkristin-chenoweth-stunned-by-talented-fan-at-hollywood-gig%2F','fb-share-dialog','width=626,height=436');" href="javascript: void(0);"><img alt="Share on Facebook" src="http://blog.sfgate.com/dailydish/wp-content/plugins/jetpack/modules/sharedaddy/images/hdn-smart-facebook.png"></a><span id="facebook_share_count_1430264578" class="facebook_share_count">0</span><script type="text/javascript">(function($) {$.getJSON('https://graph.facebook.com/?id=http://blog.sfgate.com/dailydish/2013/08/26/kristin-chenoweth-stunned-by-talented-fan-at-hollywood-gig/', function (data) { if (typeof data !== 'undefined' && data !== null && typeof data['shares'] !== 'undefined' && data['shares'] !== null) $('#facebook_share_count_1430264578').html(data['shares']); });})(jQuery);
</script></li><li class="share-twitter"><div class="twitter_button"><iframe allowtransparency="true" frameborder="0" scrolling="no" src="http://platform.twitter.com/widgets/tweet_button.html?url=http%3A%2F%2Fblog.sfgate.com%2Fdailydish%2F2013%2F08%2F26%2Fkristin-chenoweth-stunned-by-talented-fan-at-hollywood-gig%2F&#038;counturl=http%3A%2F%2Fblog.sfgate.com%2Fdailydish%2F2013%2F08%2F26%2Fkristin-chenoweth-stunned-by-talented-fan-at-hollywood-gig%2F&#038;count=horizontal&#038;text=Kristin%20Chenoweth%20stunned%20by%20talented%20fan%20at%20Hollywood%20gig%3A" style="width:86px; height:20px;"></iframe></div></li><li class="share-google-plus-1"><div class="googleplus1_button"><div class="g-plusone" data-size="medium" data-callback="sharing_plusone" data-href="http://blog.sfgate.com/dailydish/2013/08/26/kristin-chenoweth-stunned-by-talented-fan-at-hollywood-gig/"></div></div></li><li class="share-end"></li></ul></div></div></div><div id="attachment_68342" class="wp-caption alignleft" style="width: 216px"><img src="http://blog.sfgate.com/dailydish/wp-content/blogs.dir/2247/files/2013/08/kristin-206x300.jpg" alt="(Photo by Jason LaVeris/FilmMagic)" width="206" height="300" class="size-medium wp-image-68342" /><p class="wp-caption-text">(Photo by Jason LaVeris/FilmMagic)</p></div>
<p>Broadway star Kristin Chenoweth was left stunned during a show at the Hollywood Bowl in Los Angeles on Saturday when a fan joined her onstage for a &#8220;Wicked&#8221; duet and became an instant star.</p>
<p>  The actress/singer asked Sarah Horn to join her for a rendition of &#8220;For Good,&#8221; which Chenoweth sang on Broadway as a member of &#8220;Wicked&#8221;&#8216;s original cast, and was blown away by her talents.</p>
<p>  Horn, a California voice coach, belted out the duet and even harmonized with the star, leaving Chenoweth lost for words and beaming with glee.</p>
<p>  Declaring Horn&#8217;s performance &#8220;inspiring&#8221; as she left the stage to a standing ovation following her stint in the spotlight with her heroine, Chenoweth added, &#8220;That voice is teaching our young people.&#8221;</p>
<p>  Horn says her moment of glory was destined because she actually swapped seats with another concertgoer and then offered to take the place of Chenoweth&#8217;s first volunteer when she revealed she did not know the words to &#8220;For Good.&#8221;</p>
<p>  She tells LAist.com, &#8220;I lifted my microphone to my mouth, looked Kristin straight in the eye and sang the first of my lines. She leaned back and dropped her jaw. She knew I was a voice teacher but didn’t know if I did well in the execution or not. As far as she knew, I could have been tone deaf.&#8221; </p>
<p><iframe width="480" height="360" src="//www.youtube.com/embed/FpXm_sXcc_Y?rel=0" frameborder="0" allowfullscreen></iframe></p>

<p>European movie couple Monica Bellucci and Vincent Cassel have split.</p>
<p>  Italian beauty Bellucci announced on Monday that her 14-year marriage to French star Cassel was over.</p>
<p>  The couple met in 1996 on the set of acclaimed movie &#8220;l&#8217;Appartement&#8221; and wed quietly in 1999 in Monaco.</p>
<p>  Both actors have confirmed they split by &#8220;mutual agreement.&#8221;</p>
<p>  They share two daughters, Deva, 7, and Leonie, 3.</p>
<p>  The split is Bellucci&#8217;s second &#8211; she was married to photographer Claudio Basso for four years in the early 1990s.</p>

				</h2>

<p>Forest Whitaker has broken his silence about his &#8220;humiliating&#8221; shoplifting accusation in a new TV interview.</p>
<p>  The Oscar winner was mistaken for a common crook at the Milano Market in Manhattan earlier this year after a store employee suspected the actor of stealing.</p>
<p>  Embarrassed Whitaker, who was frisked in front of other shoppers, has since received an apology from the store&#8217;s owners and the &#8220;misguided&#8221; employee has been fired, but Whitaker tells ABC News film correspondent Peter Travers he&#8217;ll never forget the moment he was accused of stealing.</p>
<p>  He says, &#8220;I was angered. It&#8217;s a humiliating thing for someone to come and do that. It&#8217;s attempted dis-empowerment.&#8221;</p>
<p>  &#8220;The Butler&#8221; star adds, &#8220;Most of the stop and frisk&#8230; Nine out of the ten (times someone is frisked), the person is not a criminal. They don&#8217;t ticket them, or they don&#8217;t arrest them (and) 99 percent of them don&#8217;t have a weapon. So I think there&#8217;s something that has to be examined.&#8221; </p>

		<div class="blogitem" id="post-68331" class="post-68331 post type-post status-publish format-standard hentry category-uncategorized tag-people-you-never-thought-youd-see-in-the-dish blogentry">

					<a href="http://blog.sfgate.com/dailydish/2013/08/26/the-replacements-reunite-at-riot-fest/" title="Permalink to The Replacements reunite at Riot Fest" rel="bookmark">The Replacements reunite at Riot Fest</a>
				</h2>

						<div class="socialtools clearfix">
			
						
			<div class="count twittercontainer">
							</div>
			<div class="count facebookcontainer">
							</div>	
		</div>

							<style> .share-print{margin-right: 130px !important;}</style><div class="sharedaddy sd-sharing-enabled"><div class="robots-nocontent sd-block sd-social sd-social-official sd-sharing"><h3 class="sd-title">Share this:</h3><div class="sd-content"><ul><li class="share-comment"><a class="share-comment sd-button" href="http://blog.sfgate.com/dailydish/2013/08/26/the-replacements-reunite-at-riot-fest/?gta=commentlistpos#comments" id="cmt_count_wp_sfgate_blog_sfgate_com_dailydish_2247_blogEntryId68331_1"><span>Comments</span></a>

</li><li class="share-email"><a rel="nofollow" class="share-email sd-button" href="http://blog.sfgate.com/dailydish/2013/08/26/the-replacements-reunite-at-riot-fest/?share=email" title="Click to email this to a friend"><span>Email</span></a></li><li class="share-print"><a rel="nofollow" class="share-print sd-button" href="http://blog.sfgate.com/dailydish/2013/08/26/the-replacements-reunite-at-riot-fest/" title="Click to print"><span>Print</span></a></li><li class="share-facebook"><a onclick="javascript: window.open('https://www.facebook.com/sharer/sharer.php?u=http%3A%2F%2Fblog.sfgate.com%2Fdailydish%2F2013%2F08%2F26%2Fthe-replacements-reunite-at-riot-fest%2F','fb-share-dialog','width=626,height=436');" href="javascript: void(0);"><img alt="Share on Facebook" src="http://blog.sfgate.com/dailydish/wp-content/plugins/jetpack/modules/sharedaddy/images/hdn-smart-facebook.png"></a><span id="facebook_share_count_1472198962" class="facebook_share_count">0</span><script type="text/javascript">(function($) {$.getJSON('https://graph.facebook.com/?id=http://blog.sfgate.com/dailydish/2013/08/26/the-replacements-reunite-at-riot-fest/', function (data) { if (typeof data !== 'undefined' && data !== null && typeof data['shares'] !== 'undefined' && data['shares'] !== null) $('#facebook_share_count_1472198962').html(data['shares']); });})(jQuery);
</script></li><li class="share-twitter"><div class="twitter_button"><iframe allowtransparency="true" frameborder="0" scrolling="no" src="http://platform.twitter.com/widgets/tweet_button.html?url=http%3A%2F%2Fblog.sfgate.com%2Fdailydish%2F2013%2F08%2F26%2Fthe-replacements-reunite-at-riot-fest%2F&#038;counturl=http%3A%2F%2Fblog.sfgate.com%2Fdailydish%2F2013%2F08%2F26%2Fthe-replacements-reunite-at-riot-fest%2F&#038;count=horizontal&#038;text=The%20Replacements%20reunite%20at%20Riot%20Fest%3A" style="width:86px; height:20px;"></iframe></div></li><li class="share-google-plus-1"><div class="googleplus1_button"><div class="g-plusone" data-size="medium" data-callback="sharing_plusone" data-href="http://blog.sfgate.com/dailydish/2013/08/26/the-replacements-reunite-at-riot-fest/"></div></div></li><li class="share-end"></li></ul></div></div></div><p><iframe width="480" height="360" src="//www.youtube.com/embed/GZkrCH6jub8?rel=0" frameborder="0" allowfullscreen></iframe></p>
<p>The Replacements hit the stage at the Riot Fest in Toronto, Canada, on Sunday for their first show in over 20 years.</p>
<p>  Frontman Paul Westerberg joked about the time between gigs during the band&#8217;s headlining set, stating, &#8220;Sorry we took so long, we&#8217;ve been having a wardrobe debate &#8211; it was unresolved.&#8221;</p>
<p>  Westerberg and bassist Tommy Stinson — who were joined onstage by drummer Josh Freese and Dave Minehan on guitar — performed their first concert since an Independence Day gig in Chicago, Ill., in 1991.</p>
<p>  The duo and their new bandmates will return to that city for the next Riot Fest show on September 15 and they&#8217;ll also perform in Denver, Colo., on September 21.</p>
<p>  Westerberg and Stinson reunited last year to record the EP Songs for Slim in an effort to raise funds to help pay for former Replacements guitarist Slim Dunlap&#8217;s medical fees after he suffered a massive stroke in 2012. </p>
<p><iframe width="480" height="360" src="//www.youtube.com/embed/HsQNS6cZRus?rel=0" frameborder="0" allowfullscreen></iframe></p>
<p>Full set list:</p>
<p>Takin’ a Ride<br />
I’m in Trouble<br />
Favorite Thing<br />
Hangin’ Downtown<br />
Color Me Impressed<br />
Tommy Gets His Tonsils Out/Third Stone From the Sun (cover)<br />
Kiss Me on the Bus<br />
Androgynous<br />
Achin’ to Be<br />
I Will Dare<br />
Love You Till Friday/Maybelline (cover)<br />
Merry Go Round<br />
Wake Up<br />
Borstal Breakout (cover)<br />
Little Mascara<br />
Left of the Dial<br />
Alex Chilton<br />
Swinging Party<br />
Can’t Hardly Wait<br />
Bastards of Young </p>
<p>Everything’s Coming Up Roses (cover)<br />
I.O.U.</p>

<p>Pop star Prince was left red-faced on Friday when he forgot to stock up his wallet with cash and was unable to pay his bill at a top New York restaurant.</p>
<p>The &#8220;Purple Rain&#8221; hitmaker headed for a meal with a pal at chef Michael White&#8217;s Costata eatery but when it came time to settle the bill, he realized he had no money with him.</p>
<p>A member of Prince&#8217;s security team eventually explained the embarrassing mishap to the restaurant manager, who agreed the singer could settle the debt the following day, <a href="http://www.nypost.com/p/pagesix/purple_no_green_2IVPQiNxzljsJbk6wHONzM">according to New York Post gossip column Page Six</a>.</p>
